***toe.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a> (205)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tuo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_3">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">adverbial form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> matter.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>after, afterwards
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kreeg.html>kreeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekkers.html>lekkers</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He got something tasty <b>afterwards</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>shut, closed (especially as part of a compound verb like <a href = vnd.unilang:toedoen.html>toedoen</a>)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></b>.</i>  |  <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> closed.</i></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></b>.</i>  |  <i>Close the <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>.</i></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:oogjes.html>Oogjes</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></b>.</i>  |  <i><a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>Eyes</a> closed.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***toek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toek.html>toek</a> (78943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>An onomatopoeia.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toek.html>toek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toekennen.html>toeken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toek.html>toekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a whack or blow</li></ol>

***toen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> (121)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>doe</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></i> (with <i>-n</i> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thuo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þō</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">dunn</i> and similar forms (<i>do, du, <a href = vnd.unilang:dun.html>dun</a></i>) in German dialects.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>then, subsequently <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">at a time in the past</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>Toen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>Then</b> he left.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>back then, at the time, in those days
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>Toen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoon.html>gewoon</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>Back then</b> that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> still quite normal.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>when, at the time that <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in the past</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oud.html>oud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> vegetariër <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a>?</i>
<dl><dd>How old <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> you <b>when</b> you became vegetarian?</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>Toen</a></b> João in 1821 <a href = vnd.unilang:terugkeerde.html>terugkeerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> Portugal <a href = vnd.unilang:bleef.html>bleef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regent.html>regent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a> in Brazilië.</i>

***toentertijd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toentertijd.html>toentertijd</a> (25148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">then</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">at/on the</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> somewhat strange surprising, as it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the contraction of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> + the old feminine singular dative definite article <i><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a></i>, whereas <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a masculine word in modern Dutch. In earlier <a href = vnd.unilang:stages.html>stages</a> of the language however, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> feminine. This also explains the compound <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:indertijd.html>indertijd</a></i> and the fixed expression <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijner.html>zijner</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> which both consider <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> to be feminine, versus the younger compound <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:destijds.html>destijds</a></i> which considers it to be masculine (earliest attestation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in modern Dutch, in 1674).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toentertijd.html>toentertijd</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>at the time, then, during that time</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toentertijd.html>toentertijd</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verleden.html>verleden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelegen.html>gelegen</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toentertijd.html>toentertijd</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:besloten.html>besloten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***toer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toer.html>toer</a> (14785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:toer.html>toer</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tour</i>. Several senses are borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tour</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toer.html>toer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toeren.html>toeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toertje.html>toertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>turn, rotation, revolution</li>
<li>tour, trip</li>
<li>whim, urge <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">odd emotional action or behaviour</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>prank, <a href = vnd.unilang:stunt.html>stunt</a></li></ol>

***toeschouwer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toeschouwer.html>toeschouwer</a> (18898)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">toe-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schouwen.html>schouwen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, possibly influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zuschauer</i>. The verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">toeschouwen</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably a <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> formation.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toeschouwer.html>toeschouwer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toeschouwers.html>toeschouwers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toeschouwer.html>toeschouwertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">spectator</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toeschouwer.html>toeschouwer</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toespraak.html>toespraak</a> (4055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">toesprâke</i>. Equivalent to a deverbal of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">toespreken</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toespraak.html>toespraak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toespraken.html>toespraken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toespraakje.html>toespraakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A speech, an address.</li></ol>
